###########################
# Ireland Events
###########################

add_namespace = ire

#########################################################
### Mobilize Event (from focus)
#########################################################

country_event = {
	id = ire.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.1" }
	title = ire.1.t
	desc = ire.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_army_marching

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_manpower = -36000
		custom_effect_tooltip = "A full fighting company of eight divisions will be mobilized throughout the nation."
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE = {
				load_oob = IRE_MOBILIZE_FULL
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_manpower = -18000
		custom_effect_tooltip = "A half-strength fighting company of four divisions will be mobilized throughout the nation."
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE = {
				load_oob = IRE_MOBILIZE_HALF
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.1.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_manpower = -9000
		custom_effect_tooltip = "A reserve infantry company of two divisions will be mobilized in Dublin and Belfast."
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE = {
				load_oob = IRE_MOBILIZE_WEAK
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hidden event to start tension mechanics
country_event = {
	id = ire.3000
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.3000" }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		set_country_flag = IRE_ulster_conflict
		country_event = { id = ire.3 days = 30 }
	}
}
# Hidden event to fire tension events
country_event = {
	id = ire.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.3000" }
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = IRE_ulster_conflict
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = ire.3 days = 20 random_days = 80 }
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_factory_clash_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_factory_clash_event
		country_event = ire.43
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = IRE_factory_clash_event
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_UVF_shooting_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_UVF_shooting_event
		country_event = ire.44
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = IRE_UVF_shooting_event
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_antrim_concert_shooting_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_antrim_concert_shooting_event
		country_event = ire.46
	}

	option = {

	}

	option = {

			check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation > 1 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_belfast_city_hall_bombing_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_belfast_city_hall_bombing_event
		country_event = ire.49
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation > 1 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_grand_opera_house_fire_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_grand_opera_house_fire_event
		country_event = ire.50
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_bank_robbery_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_bank_robbery_event
		country_event = ire.51
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation > 2 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_dublin_bombing_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_dublin_bombing_event
		country_event = ire.52
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_war = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_pushing_for_independence_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_pushing_for_independence_event
		country_event = ire.58
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_war = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		set_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
		country_event = ire.36
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { ire_unionist_tensions > 19 }
			check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation > 3 }
			owns_state = 119
			controls_all_owned_states = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = IRE_ulster_conflict
		country_event = ire.133 #Civil War
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation = 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.625
				check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = ire.36.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.36.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		increase_unionist_tensions = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE = {
				country_event = {
					id = ire.63
					days = 35
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.36.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE = {
				country_event = {
					id = ire.37
					days = 35
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Deploying Soldiers

country_event = {
	id = ire.39
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.39" }
	title = ire.39.t
	desc = ire.39.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_occupation

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.39.a
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_michael_collins = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Eoin_O'Duffy_dead }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		set_country_flag = ire_oduffy_in_charge
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.39.b
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_michael_collins = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		set_country_flag = ire_mulcahy_in_charge
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.39.c
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_michael_collins = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		set_country_flag = ire_lynch_in_charge
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.39.e
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_michael_collins = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}

}

# Unionist Protest March 3

country_event = {
	id = ire.38
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.38" }
	title = ire.38.t

	desc = {
		text = ire.38.d
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ire_march_notroops
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = ire.38.d2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ire_oduffy_in_charge
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = ire.38.d3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ire_mulcahy_in_charge
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ire.38.d4
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ire_lynch_in_charge
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ire.38.d5
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ire_macneill_in_charge
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.42" }

	desc = ire.42.d

		name = ire.42.a

			factor = 50
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		reduce_unionist_tensions = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = ire.42.oduffy.imprisoned
		set_country_flag = Eoin_O'Duffy_dead

			limit = { has_unit_leader = 9911 }
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 9911 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = IRE_Eoin_O'Duffy_carm_pau }
			remove_ideas = IRE_Eoin_O'Duffy_carm_pau
		}

			remove_ideas = {
				IRE_Eoin_O'Duffy_hog_pau

			}

		}

		reduce_unionist_tensions = yes

country_event = { #Unionist Uprising
	id = ire.133
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.133" }
	title = ire.133.t
	desc = ire.133.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_civil_war

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ULS = {
				add_state_core = 119 #Ulster
				transfer_state = 119
				transfer_technology = yes
				add_ideas = {
					ULS_CATHOLICS
					partial_economic_mobilisation
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = ULS_NO_SURRENDER days = 365 }
				division_template = {
					name = "Ulster Volunteers"
					division_names_group = ULS_MIL_01
					regiments = {
						militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						militia = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 2 y = 2 }
						militia = { x = 3 y = 0 }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ire.151 days = 365 } #Peace with Ireland?
			}
			119 = {
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ally_with = ROOT
							has_military_access_to = ROOT
						}
					}
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Ulster Volunteers\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
					owner = ULS
					count = 5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_KILLUVF }
				ULS = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ULS_WEAKENED4 days = 365 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_REOCCBF }
				ULS = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ULS_WEAKENED3 days = 365 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_RTUG }
				ULS = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ULS_WEAKENED2 days = 365 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_REPRESS }
				ULS = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ULS_WEAKENED1 days = 365 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.133.a
		add_political_power = -100
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ULS
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ire.133.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		add_political_power = -100
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ULS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		ULS = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

# Yearly Immigration Waves
# Three 'levels' deciding population income. Low world tension, high world tension, and Ireland's war status (being at war dramatically reduces immigration for obvious reasons)

country_event = {
	id = ire.98
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.98 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ire.98.t
	#LWT
	desc = {
		text = ire.98.d
		trigger = {
			has_war = no
			threat < 0.5
		}
	}
	#HWT
	desc = {
		text = ire.98.d2
		trigger = {
			has_war = no
			threat > 0.5
		}
	}
	#IW
	desc = {
		text = ire.98.d3
		trigger = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_immigration

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = IRE_EIE
		check_variable = { IRE_immigration_year < global.year } #to avoid firing multiple times per year
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { IRE_immigration_year = global.year }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ire.98 days = 365 }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.98.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 2 } }
				119 = { add_manpower = 7233 }
				134 = { add_manpower = 5541 }
				135 = { add_manpower = 3603 }
				113 = { add_manpower = 4921 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 1 } }
				119 = { add_manpower = 3465 }
				134 = { add_manpower = 2478 }
				135 = { add_manpower = 4532 }
				113 = { add_manpower = 3105 }
			}
			else = {
				119 = { add_manpower = 3250 }
				134 = { add_manpower = 198 }
				135 = { add_manpower = 1732 }
				113 = { add_manpower = 4070 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { threat > 0.5 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 2 } }
					119 = { add_manpower = 64500 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 25402 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 21510 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 41705 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 1 } }
					119 = { add_manpower = 17150 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 16623 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 14291 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 13032 }
				}
				else = {
					119 = { add_manpower = 9412 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 9420 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 8953 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 11550 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 2 } }
					119 = { add_manpower = 14335 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 16205 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 15503 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 18023 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 1 } }
					119 = { add_manpower = 8232 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 7405 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 7721 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 8712 }
				}
				else = {
					119 = { add_manpower = 3456 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 4321 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 3621 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 5251 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# 1937 Elections
country_event = {
	id = ire.14
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.14"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = IRE_1937_elections
		}
	}
	title = ire.14.t
	desc = ire.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_collins_speech1
	
	trigger = {
		IRE_has_michael_collins = yes
		date < 1938.1.1
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Collins wins!
		name = ire.14.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = IRE_future
						option = IRE_FUTURE_PATAUT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = IRE_future
						option = IRE_FUTURE_DEMOCRACY_SOCCON
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = IRE_future
						option = IRE_FUTURE_DEMOCRACY_MARLIB
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = IRE_future
						option = IRE_FUTURE_DEMOCRACY_SOCLIB
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = IRE_future
						option = IRE_FUTURE_DEMOCRACY_SOCDEM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = IRE_future
						option = IRE_FUTURE_SYNDIE
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = IRE_Eoin_O'Duffy_hog_pau
					}

				add_ideas = {
					IRE_Eoin_O'Duffy_hog_pau

				}
			}
			news_event = {
				id = ire.360
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # SocDems
		name = ire.14.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = IRE_future
						option = IRE_FUTURE_AUTHDEM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = IRE_future
						option = IRE_FUTURE_SYNDIE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = IRE_future
						option = IRE_FUTURE_PATAUT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_SOCDEMS_WIN
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				IRE_Thomas_Johnson_hog_sde
				IRE_Sean_MacBride_for_sde
				IRE_William_Norton_eco_sde
				IRE_Liam_Mellows_sec_sde
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ire.252
				days = 20
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ire.318
				days = 76
			}
			
		}
		hidden_effect = {

				id = ire.361
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}

				name = IRE_social_democrat_party

			}
			set_variable = {
				current_FG_pop = party_popularity@market_liberal
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_SF_pop = party_popularity@social_democrat
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_FG_pop
				value = current_SF_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = current_FG_pop
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes

		text = ire.17.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { 
		text = ire.17.d.pataut
		trigger = {
			has_government = paternal_autocrat
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_collins_speech1

		IRE_has_michael_collins = yes
		date > 1938.1.1
		date < 1943.1.1
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

			}
		}

				has_government = market_liberal 
			}

			}
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
	
	option = {

			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes

				IRE_Sean_MacBride_for_sde

		}
	}

			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }

			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				IRE_James_Dillon_hog_sli
				IRE_John_O'Hanlon_for_sli

				IRE_Patrick_Baxter_sec_sli
			}
		}

	}

		}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.220" }
	title = ire.220.t
	desc = ire.220.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_communists_cheer

	trigger = {
		has_socialist_government = yes
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.220.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_acs_language_rwg
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = IRE_acs_rwg
			value = 1
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		increase_unionist_tensions = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ire.220.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_acs_language_iwl
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = IRE_acs_iwl
			value = 1
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ire.220.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_acs_language_se
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = IRE_acs_se
			value = 1
		}
		add_ideas = IRE_GAELIC
		add_political_power = -50
		increase_unionist_tensions = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ire.220.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_acs_language_labour
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = IRE_acs_labour
			value = 1
		}
		add_ideas = IRE_GAELIC
		add_political_power = -50
		increase_unionist_tensions = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
}

# RWG Victory

country_event = {
	id = ire.224
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.224" }
	title = ire.224.t
	desc = ire.224.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		tag = IRE
		has_socialist_government = yes
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = IRE_acs_rwg
			value > 2
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.224.a
		remove_all_ministers = yes

		add_ideas = {
			IRE_Jim_Gralton_hog_tot
			IRE_Benjamin_Farrington_for_tot
			IRE_Robert_N_Tweedy_eco_tot
			IRE_James_Everett_sec_tot
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
	}
}

# Dail

country_event = {
	id = ire.2271
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.2271" }
	title = ire.2271.t
	desc = ire.2271.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_larkin

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.2271.a
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Revolutionary Dáil"
			desc = "POLITICS_DAIL_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/IRE/Portrait_Ireland_Revolutionary_Dail.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = centralized_syndicalism_subtype
		}
		add_ideas = IRE_anti_socialist_resistance
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				name = IRE_social_democrat_party2
				long_name = IRE_social_democrat_party2_long
				ideology = social_democrat
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "William X. O'Brien"
				desc = "POLITICS_WILLIAM_X_OBRIEN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/IRE/Portrait_Ireland_William_X_O'Brien.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = syndie_social_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Black Monday hits Ireland!
	id = ire.228
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.228" }
	title = ire.228.t
	desc = ire.228.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_dail_meeting

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.228.a
		add_political_power = -150
		add_ideas = IRE_black_monday_1
		set_country_flag = IRE_black_monday
	}
}

country_event = { #The Emergency
	id = ire.2511
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.2511" }
	title = ire.2511.t
	desc = ire.2511.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_valera
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Éamon de Valera"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Extend Valera's authority
		name = ire.2511.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_FF_Authdem
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.3
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_IRE_soccon_pop = party_popularity@social_conservative
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_IRE_authdem_pop = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_IRE_soccon_pop
				value = current_IRE_authdem_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = current_IRE_soccon_pop
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_FF_AUTH
	}
	
	option = { #nah
		name = ire.2511.b
		add_stability = 0.02
	}
}

country_event = { #Pan Celtic Dream
	id = ire.304
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.304" }
	title = ire.304.t
	desc = ire.304.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_pan_celtic
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_government = national_populist
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_ideology = integralism_subtype
				has_country_leader_ideology = occultism_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = ire.304.a
		#Isolation
		set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_CELT2
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = IRE_isolation
				}
			}
			add_ideas = IRE_isolation
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = ire.304.b
		set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_CELT
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = ICE
					is_core_of = POR
				}
			}
			IRE = {
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		add_state_core = 983
		add_state_core = 14
		add_state_core = 171
		create_wargoal = {
               target = ICE
               type = annex_everything
            }
		create_wargoal = {
               target = POR
               type = annex_everything
            }
		create_wargoal = {
               target = 983.owner
               type = annex_everything
            }
		create_wargoal = {
               target = 14.owner
               type = annex_everything
            }	
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = ire.304.c
		set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_CELT3
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = ICE
					is_core_of = POR
					is_core_of = SPR
					is_core_of = CNT
					is_core_of = CAR
					is_core_of = FRA
					is_core_of = SWI
					is_core_of = BEL
					is_core_of = HOL
					is_core_of = GER
					is_core_of = ITA
					is_core_of = AUS
					is_core_of = CZE
					is_core_of = CRO
					is_core_of = GAL
					is_core_of = HUN
					is_core_of = SER
					is_core_of = ROM
					is_core_of = BUL
					is_core_of = TUR
					is_core_of = SLO

				}
			}
			IRE = {
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		add_state_core = 983
		add_state_core = 14
		create_wargoal = {
               target = ICE
               type = annex_everything
            }
		create_wargoal = {
               target = POR

            }

		name = ire.331.b

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = national_populist
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = national_populist
				}
				set_variable = {
					current_IRE_soccon_pop = party_popularity@social_conservative
				}
				set_variable = {
					current_IRE_natpop_pop = party_popularity@national_populist
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = current_IRE_soccon_pop
					value = current_IRE_natpop_pop
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = national_populist
					popularity = current_IRE_soccon_pop
				}
				set_party_name = {
					name = IRE_authoritarian_democrat_party
					long_name = IRE_authoritarian_democrat_party_long
					ideology = national_populist
				}
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = occultism_subtype
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_FF_NATPOP
	}	
	
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_london
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = IRE
		OR = {
			owns_state = 126
			GBP = {
				owns_state = 126
				is_subject_of = IRE
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.345.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event=  {
				id = ire.365
				days = 15
			}
			every_state = {
			limit = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_owned_by = IRE
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = SCT
							is_core_of = WAL
							is_core_of = IRE
						}
					}
			}
			GBP = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		IRE = {
			puppet = GBP
		}
		GBP = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GBP_REPUBLIC
			country_event = {
				id = part.64
				days = 2
			}
		}
		}
	}	
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.345.b
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event=  {
				id = ire.365
				days = 15
			}
			every_state = {
			limit = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_owned_by = IRE
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = SCT
							is_core_of = WAL
							is_core_of = IRE
						}
					}
			}
			add_core_of = GBP
			GBP = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		IRE = {
			puppet = GBP
		}
		GBP = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GBP_FREESTATE
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			}
			create_country_leader = {
			name = "Executive Council"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/IRE/Portrait_Ireland_English_Exe_Council.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = junta_subtype
			}
		}
		}
		
	}
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.345.c
		add_timed_idea = { idea = IRE_BRTISHARMY days = 800 } 
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ENG
			}
			add_core_of = IRE
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GBP = {
					is_subject_of = IRE
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
			target = GBP
			transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event=  {
				id = ire.365
				days = 15
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ire.341
				days = 35
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.345.e
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 126
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		country_event=  {
				id = ire.365
				days = 15
			}
	}

country_event = { #French said yes to peace
	id = ire.354
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.343" }
	title = ire.354.t
	desc = ire.354.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_no_english
	

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.354.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = ENG
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_core_of = WAL
					is_core_of = SCT
					is_core_of = IRE
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		IRE = {
			annex_country = {
			target = ENG
			transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SCT = {
					exists = yes
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
			}
			IRE = {
				annex_country = {
					target = SCT
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				WAL = {
					exists = yes
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
			}
			IRE = {
				annex_country = {
					target = WAL
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = IRE
				OR = {
					tag = FRA
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
			}
			white_peace = IRE
		}	
	}								
}

country_event = { #Integralism?
	id = ire_monarch.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire_monarch.6" }
	title = ire_monarch.6.t
	desc = ire_monarch.6.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_kingdom_coa
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Integralism
		name = ire_monarch.6.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25 
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_country_flag = IRE_King_Hugo
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_FF_Natpop
		hidden_effect = {

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_populist
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_IRE_soccon_pop = party_popularity@social_conservative
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_IRE_natpop_pop = party_popularity@national_populist
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_IRE_soccon_pop
				value = current_IRE_natpop_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = current_IRE_soccon_pop
			}
			set_party_name = {
				name = IRE_authoritarian_democrat_party
				long_name = IRE_authoritarian_democrat_party_long
				ideology = national_populist
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ire_monarch.11
				days = 22
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_FF_NATPOP
	}
	
	option = { # Constitutonalism
		name = ire_monarch.6.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75 
		}
		add_political_power = 40
	}
	
}
